        }

          width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://crrev.com/31e17fe62d59968f6f89f5c33eaf8fa75d375b77"><!---->31e17fe62d59968f6f89f5c33eaf8fa75d375b77<!----></a>

<span class="line"><!---->    [shared-struct, api] Support shared isolates in API<!----></span>

with need "--harmony-struct", acitive release: M113/dev, M112/beta, M111/stable



<span class="line"><!---->with need "--harmony-struct", acitive release: M113/dev, M112/beta, M111/stable<!----></span>

bug details 



<span class="line"><!---->bug details <!----></span>



<br>





when `FlatStringReader::Get` try to get a char from heap which saved a string need simplify, the heap seem be clear or freed, then lead to egmentation fault [1]



<span class="line"><!---->when `FlatStringReader::Get` try to get a char from heap which saved a string need simplify, the heap seem be clear or freed, then lead to egmentation fault [1]<!----></span>



<br>





```



<span class="line"><!---->```<!----></span>

Char FlatStringReader::Get(int index) const {



<span class="line"><!---->Char FlatStringReader::Get(int index) const {<!----></span>



<br>





  DCHECK_EQ(is_one_byte_, sizeof(Char) == 1);



<span class="line"><!---->  DCHECK_EQ(is_one_byte_, sizeof(Char) == 1);<!----></span>



<br>





  DCHECK(0 <= index && index < length_);



<span class="line"><!---->  DCHECK(0 &lt;= index &amp;&amp; index &lt; length_);<!----></span>

  if (sizeof(Char) == 1) {



<span class="line"><!---->  if (sizeof(Char) == 1) {<!----></span>



<br>





    return static_cast<Char>(static_cast<const uint8_t*>(start_)[index]);    <----------------------



<span class="line"><!---->    return static_cast&lt;Char&gt;(static_cast&lt;const uint8_t*&gt;(start_)[index]);    &lt;----------------------<!----></span>

  } else {



<span class="line"><!---->  } else {<!----></span>



<br>





    return static_cast<Char>(static_cast<const base::uc16*>(start_)[index]);



<span class="line"><!---->    return static_cast&lt;Char&gt;(static_cast&lt;const base::uc16*&gt;(start_)[index]);<!----></span>

  }

[heap] Disable black allocation in shared heap during client GC



<span class="line"><!---->[heap] Disable black allocation in shared heap during client GC<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





A scavenger GC can run on a client isolate while incremental marking



<span class="line"><!---->A scavenger GC can run on a client isolate while incremental marking<!----></span>



<br>





is enabled in the shared space isolate. While we pause black



<span class="line"><!---->is enabled in the shared space isolate. While we pause black<!----></span>



<br>





allocation in the client's heap, we can't really pause it in the



<span class="line"><!---->allocation in the client's heap, we can't really pause it in the<!----></span>



<br>





shared heap isolate.



<span class="line"><!---->shared heap isolate.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





This CL solves that by marking ConcurrentAllocator instances created



<span class="line"><!---->This CL solves that by marking ConcurrentAllocator instances created<!----></span>



<br>





for the GC. Black allocation is never enabled during GC. This will



<span class="line"><!---->for the GC. Black allocation is never enabled during GC. This will<!----></span>



<br>





probably also be useful when moving LABs out of the spaces.



<span class="line"><!---->probably also be useful when moving LABs out of the spaces.<!----></span>

<span class="line"><!---->only for the main isolate but also the client isolates.<!----></span>

space string on its own isolate. When a shared GC then happens while

<span class="line"><!---->the FlatStringReader is still active, the shared GC also needs to<!----></span>

To clarify the non-experimental state of --shared-string-table:



<span class="line"><!---->To clarify the non-experimental state of --shared-string-table:<!----></span>



<br>





While --harmony-struct implies --shared-string-table and --harmony-struct is considered experimental, --shared-string-table is considered ready and we are happy about external reports.



<span class="line"><!---->While --harmony-struct implies --shared-string-table and --harmony-struct is considered experimental, --shared-string-table is considered ready and we are happy about external reports.<!----></span>



<br>





Bugs that only require --shared-string-table (without --harmony-struct) should be considered for VRP rewards.



<span class="line"><!---->Bugs that only require --shared-string-table (without --harmony-struct) should be considered for VRP rewards.<!----></span>

*** Boilerplate reminders! ***



<span class="line"><!---->*** Boilerplate reminders! ***<!----></span>



<br>





Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward. Also, please be considerate about disclosure when the bug affects a core library that may be used by other products. Please do NOT share this information with third parties who are not directly involved in fixing the bug. Doing so may cancel the provisional reward. Please be honest if you have already disclosed anything publicly or to third parties. Lastly, we understand that some of you are not interested in money. We offer the option to donate your reward to an eligible charity. If you prefer this option, let us know and we will also match your donation - subject to our discretion. Any rewards that are unclaimed after 12 months will be donated to a charity of our choosing.



<span class="line"><!---->Please do NOT publicly disclose details until a fix has been released to all our users. Early public disclosure may cancel the provisional reward.
